function update_all_ranges
	lowest1{int} {lowest1}  := 128
	highest1{int} {highest1}  := 0
	i4{int} {i4}  := 0
	while(i4{int} {i4}  <= 0) 
		instrument1{int} {instrument1}  := i4{int} {i4} 
		lowest0{int} {lowest0}  := 128
		highest0{int} {highest0}  := 0
		s0{int} {s0}  := 0
		ks0{int} {ks0}  := 0
		while(ks0{int} {ks0}  <= 7) 
			if(_keyswitch_states[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 8) + ks0{int} {ks0} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  = 1)
				s0{int} {s0}  := 0
				while(s0{int} {s0}  <= 3) 
					if(_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 32) + ((ks0{int} {ks0}  * 4) + s0{int} {s0} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  >= 0)
						if(subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 32) + ((ks0{int} {ks0}  * 4) + s0{int} {s0} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower}  < lowest0{int} {lowest0} )
							lowest0{int} {lowest0}  := subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 32) + ((ks0{int} {ks0}  * 4) + s0{int} {s0} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower} 
						end if
						if(subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 32) + ((ks0{int} {ks0}  * 4) + s0{int} {s0} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper}  > highest0{int} {highest0} )
							highest0{int} {highest0}  := subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 32) + ((ks0{int} {ks0}  * 4) + s0{int} {s0} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper} 
						end if
					end if
					inc(s0{int} {s0} ){Builtin, None}
				end while
			end if
			inc(ks0{int} {ks0} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		_instrument_range[instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 2]{int} {_instrument_range}  := (lowest0{int} {lowest0}  - range_offset_lower{int} {range_offset_lower} ) - (octave_shift[instrument1{int} {instrument1} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
		_instrument_range[(instrument1{int} {instrument1}  * 2) + 1]{int} {_instrument_range}  := (highest0{int} {highest0}  + range_offset_upper{int} {range_offset_upper} ) - (octave_shift[instrument1{int} {instrument1} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
		lowest1{int} {lowest1}  := lowest1{int} {lowest1}  - ((lowest1{int} {lowest1}  - _instrument_range[i4{int} {i4}  * 2]{int} {_instrument_range} ) .and. sh_right(_instrument_range[i4{int} {i4}  * 2]{int} {_instrument_range}  - lowest1{int} {lowest1} , 31){Builtin, None})

		inc(i4{int} {i4} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range}  := lowest1{int} {lowest1} 
	nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range}  := highest1{int} {highest1} 
	transition0{int} {transition0}  := 0
	while(transition0{int} {transition0}  <= 127) 
		set_key_color(transition0{int} {transition0} , KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int} {KEY_COLOR_WHITE} ){Builtin, None}
		if((transition0{int} {transition0}  >= nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range} ) and (transition0{int} {transition0}  <= nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range} ))
			set_key_color(transition0{int} {transition0} , KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int} {KEY_COLOR_BLUE} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(transition0{int} {transition0} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= 7) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_RED{int} {KEY_COLOR_RED} ){Builtin, None}

		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function delay_buffer_add

function articulations_note_off

		while(i10{int} {i10}  <= 3)

			end if
		end if
		inc(i12{int} {i12} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function subarticulation_group_count
	stop_voice0{int} {stop_voice0}  := 0
	if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = 2)
		stop_voice0{int} {stop_voice0}  := 6 * ((subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_dynamic_layers}  * 3) + subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_trans_num} )
	else
		stop_voice0{int} {stop_voice0}  := (6 * subarticulations_interval_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_interval_num} ) * ((subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_rr_num}  * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_dynamic_layers} ) * (1 + subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_event_id13{int} {subarticulation_event_id13} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_release_group} ))
	end if
	fade_time1{int} {fade_time1}  := stop_voice0{int} {stop_voice0} 
end function

function set_key_colors
	transition0{int} {transition0}  := 0
	while(transition0{int} {transition0}  <= 127) 
		set_key_color(transition0{int} {transition0} , KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int} {KEY_COLOR_WHITE} ){Builtin, None}
		if((transition0{int} {transition0}  >= nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range} ) and (transition0{int} {transition0}  <= nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range} ))
			set_key_color(transition0{int} {transition0} , KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int} {KEY_COLOR_BLUE} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(transition0{int} {transition0} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= 7) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_RED{int} {KEY_COLOR_RED} ){Builtin, None}
		if(_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  = 1)
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int} {KEY_COLOR_ORANGE} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 0
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # -1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = 2)
			authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 1
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int} {lbl_authoring_legato_title} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name}  & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function authoring_open
	call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, Call}
	ret6{int} {ret6}  := 60
	idx2100{int} {idx2100}  := 60
	instrument8{int} {instrument8}  := 0
	call update_authoring_transition{UserDefined, Call}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_authoring{int} {pnl_authoring} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
end function

end function

function center_circle_distance
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00}  - 0.5
	transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength00{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength00}  - 0.5
	subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0}  := sqrt((subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  * subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} ) + (transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  * transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0} )){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle
	transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  - 0.5
	subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength00{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength00}  - 0.5
	cos_theta0{real} {cos_theta0}  := transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00}  / sqrt((transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00}  * transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00} ) + (subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0}  * subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0} )){Builtin, None}
	angle1{real} {angle1}  := acos(cos_theta0{real} {cos_theta0} ){Builtin, None}
	if(subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0}  < 0)
		angle1{real} {angle1}  := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} ) - angle1{real} {angle1} 
	end if
	transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  := angle1{real} {angle1} 
end function

function angle_to_value
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength0}  + (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  / 2)
	if(subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  > (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2))
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )
	end if
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := abs(subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )){Builtin, None}
	keyswitch10{int} {keyswitch10}  := int((127 * (subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  - transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00} )) / (subarticulation_modulation_strength00{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength00}  - transition_speed00{real} {transition_speed00} )){Builtin, None}
end function
